         </picture>

        <div class="c-stage__item__wrapper c-stage__item__wrapper--bottom row">
         <div class="c-stage__item--content">
          <h3 class="c-stage__item--title large ">
          </h3>
          <p>
           Helicopters
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
    </div>
    <div class="row clear-padding">
     <div class="introcontainer parbase has-padding col-xs-12 col-sm-12 no-margin-bottom">
      <div class="c-introcontainer c-introcontainer--white row has-padding" data-analytics-component-name="introcontainer" data-analytics-component-title="introcontainer" style="background-color:  #708cb3">
       <div class="col-sm-8">
        <div class="row">
         <div class="text parbase col-sm-offset-2 has-padding col-xs-12 col-sm-12 no-margin-bottom">
          <div class="c-text">
           <p>
            Airbus strives to provide the most efficient helicopter solutions to its customers who serve, protect, save lives and safely carry passengers in demanding environments. Its helicopters are in service across more than 150 countries worldwide, performing nearly every type of vertical flight task imaginable. The company’s product line offers the full spectrum of rotary-wing aircraft solutions for civil, government, military, law enforcement and parapublic uses.
           </p>
           <p>
            Its civilian helicopters range from the light single-engine H125 to the 11-ton twin-turbine H225 rotorcraft. Military versions are mission-proven in the most demanding front-line conditions, and are trusted by more than 160 armed forces worldwide.
           </p>
           <p>
            Safety is at the core of all Airbus’ activities. From design, engineering and production, to maintenance, training and partnerships, Airbus is focused on meeting and exceeding industry safety standards and supporting the flight safety for the thousands of men and women around the world who are transported in its aircraft every day.
            <br/>
           </p>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="col-sm-4">
        <div class="row">
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
    </div>

     <div class="titlelarge title parbase col-sm-offset-2 col-sm-8 col-xs-12 has-padding-left no-margin-bottom">
      <div class="c-titlelarge">
       <p>
        HCare service offer
       </p>
      </div>
     </div>
    </div>
    <div class="row">
     <div class="parbase textmediaparagraph has-padding col-xs-12 col-sm-12">
      <div class="c-textmediaparagraph row reorder-xs cq-dd-image" data-analytics-component-name="Text Media Paragraph" data-analytics-component-title="Text Media Paragraph">
       <div class="col-sm-6 media-wrapper pull-left">
       </div>
       <div class="col-sm-offset-2 col-sm-8 text-wrapper text">
        <p>
         The moment an Airbus helicopter is delivered, one of the company’s primary missions begins: providing the customer with the necessary support and services to carry out their operations efficiently, safely and cost-effectively.
        </p>
        <p>
         Airbus Helicopters’ global Customer Services network works around the clock to fulfill this mission, bringing tailor-made and competitive solutions to the customer’s doorstep.
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="/helicopters/services.html">
          Visit our helicopter services page
         </a>
        </p>

     <div class="titlelarge title parbase col-sm-offset-2 col-sm-8 col-xs-12 has-padding-left no-margin-bottom">
      <div class="c-titlelarge">
       <a name="missions">
       </a>
       <p>
        Missions. Behind the scenes
       </p>
      </div>
     </div>
    </div>
    <div class="row">
     <div class="parbase textmediaparagraph has-padding col-xs-12 col-sm-12">
      <div class="c-textmediaparagraph row reorder-xs cq-dd-image" data-analytics-component-name="Text Media Paragraph" data-analytics-component-title="Text Media Paragraph">
       <div class="col-sm-6 media-wrapper pull-left">
       </div>
       <div class="col-sm-offset-2 col-sm-8 text-wrapper text">
        <p>
         As the world’s No.1 helicopter manufacturer, Airbus provides the most efficient civil and military helicopter solutions to our customers who serve, protect, save lives and safely carry passengers in highly demanding environments.
         <br/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Airbus helicopters are deployed on missions worldwide for diverse aerial duties.
         <br/>
        </p>

             <div class="c-media__chapo link--lightbox">
              <p class="c-media__chapo__txt">
               The Guangzhou Public Security Bureau in Guangdong Province, China, has ordered a second H145 for delivery in 2019 to perform public service missions including passenger transport, search and rescue, and traffic surveillance and intervention. In December 2016, the bureau introduced the first fully police-equipped H145 in China, accumulating 500 flight hours in one year and a half. In China today, more than 20 Airbus helicopters are operated by over nine police bureaus, including Guangdong, Guangzhou, Shanghai, Dalian, Wuhan, Shaanxi, Fuzhou, Shenyang and Hong Kong.
              </p>

             <div class="c-media__chapo link--lightbox">
              <p class="c-media__chapo__txt">
               A medical team from non-profit organisation Boston MedFlight transports a patient with an H145 helicopter in Eastern Massachusetts. Boston MedFlight has flown Airbus helicopters since the its founding in 1985. Originally created to rapidly transport patients with life threatening illnesses, Boston MedFlight has evolved into a critical care transport system for critically ill and injured patients in the region.
              </p>

              <p class="c-media__chapo__txt">
               For the full complement of airborne law enforcement missions – including those performed with city, state or highway police; carried out by customs, border patrol, and coast guard units; and implemented by drug enforcement, SWAT or search teams – Airbus provides the helicopters, capability and special equipment to get the job done – no matter how complex the task.

         t.src = '//assetscdn.stackla.com/media/js/widget/fluid-embed.js';
         t.id = id;
         (d.getElementsByTagName('head')[0] || d.getElementsByTagName('body')[0]).appendChild(t);
     }(document, 'stackla-widget-js'));
      </script>
     </div>
    </div>
